2a1(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / 'phags pa nyan thos thams
2a2(sna tshogs): cad la phyag 'tshal lo// 'di skad bdag gis thos pa dus gcig na/ bcom ldan 'das rgyal
2a3(sna tshogs): po'i 'ang na/ 'od ma'i tshal bya ka lan trag gnas pa na/ dge slong stong nyis brgya lnga bcu'i dge slong
2a4(sna tshogs): gi dge 'dun chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing tha
2b1(sna tshogs): dad pa nas 'dus pa/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa tshad med grangs med pa dang thabs cig tu bzhugs te/ de'i tshe bcom
2b2(sna tshogs): ldan 'das 'khor brgya stong du mas yongs su bskor cing mdun gyis bltas te chos ston to// de nas byang chub
2b3(sna tshogs): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa zhes bya ba 'khor de nyid du 'dus par gyur nas 'dug
2b4(sna tshogs): pa de stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs te/ bcom
2b5(sna tshogs): ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar ba btud nas/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// gal te zhus
3a1(sna tshogs): nas zhu ba lung bstan pa'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag la skabs phyer/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom
3a2(sna tshogs): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la bdag phyogs 'ga' zhig zhu lags so// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis
3a3(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam
3a4(sna tshogs): par gnon pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la khyod ci dang ci 'dod pa dris shig dang / dris
3a5(sna tshogs): pa de dang de'i lung bstan pas khyod kyi sems rangs par bya'o// de skad ces bka' skul pa dang // bcom ldan 'das la
3a6(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das shes rab kyi pha
3b1(sna tshogs): rol tu phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bgyi ba/ bcom ldan 'das ji tsam gyis na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes gyi/
3b2(sna tshogs): bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la spyod pa lags/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa
3b3(sna tshogs): la stod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgom pa yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan 'das ji ltar na byang chub sems
3b4(sna tshogs): dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsgob pa na/ bdud ldog can gyis glags mi rnyed cing / bdud kyi las thams cad kyang rtogs par 'gyur ba lags/ bcom ldan
3b5(sna tshogs): 'das byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la gnas pa ji lta bus gnas na/ myur du thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi chos yongs su rdzogs par 'gyur
3b6(sna tshogs): ba lags/ de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces
3b7(sna tshogs): bka' stsal to// rab kyi tshul gyis rnam par gnon pa khyod/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi don dang / ci nas khyod skye bo mang po la phan pa dang /
4a1(sna tshogs): mang po bde ba dang / 'jig rten la snying brtse ba dang / lnga dang mi rnams kyi skye bo phal po chu'i don dang / pan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir zhus shing / da ltar
4a2(sna tshogs): gyi dang / ma 'ongs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams la snang ba byed par 'dod pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la/
4a3(sna tshogs): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'dri ba legs so legs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis mkhyen bzhin du/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal
4a4(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rab kyi rtsal gyi rnam par gnon pa khyod don gyi dbang gang mthong nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa la don 'di lta bu 'dri/
4a5(sna tshogs): de skad ces bka' stsal pa dang / bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pas 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom
4a6(sna tshogs): ldan 'das sems can thams cad la sman pa dang / sems can thams cad la snying brtse ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi don gyi slad du/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la
4a7(sna tshogs): ngor 'di zhu lags so// de ci'i slang du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das 'di lta ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang / byang chub
4b1(sna tshogs): sems dpa' dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos dang / chos thams cad snang pa lags pa'i slang du'o// bcom ldan 'das de la sems can gang dag
4b2(sna tshogs): thos kyi theg pa la nges par gyur pa de dag gis thos na myur du zag pa ma mchis pa'i sa mngon sum du bgyid par 'gyur ba dang / gang dag rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la nges par gyur pa de
4b3(sna tshogs): ngag kyang myur du rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pas nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ba dang / gang dag bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la yang dag par zhugs pa de dag kyang myur du zun
4b4(sna tshogs): meng pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba dang / gang dag yang dag pa nyid skyon med pa la ma zhugs shing sa gsum la ma nges pa de dag gis thos
4b5(sna tshogs): dathar med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par 'gyur ba dang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di zhus pa'i la par
4b6(sna tshogs): pas sems can thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed par 'gyur ba'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i yul dung de bzhir gshegs pa'i ye shes bstan du gsol/ bcom ldan 'das
4b7(sna tshogs): dngag ni sems car sman pa la mos pa rnams kyi sred du/ de ba'ir gshegs pa la zhung ma legs/ dbul ba'i sems dang ldan pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ dbul po'i theg pa la yang
5a1(sna tshogs): dag par zhugs pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ le lo car rnams kyi slad du ma lagasale lo'i zil gyis non pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ lta ba'i 'dab du bying /
5a2(sna tshogs): ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags// bdud kyi zhags pas zin pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ ngo tsha ma 'tshal cing khrel ma mchis pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ yo byad bsnyungs pa dang mi
5a3(sna tshogs): ldan pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags// bskyung ngas pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ sems 'khrul pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ 'dod pa'i 'dam du bying ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags
5a4(sna tshogs): g.yon can rnams kyi slad du ma lags sgyu can rnams kyi slad du ma lags bgyis pa mi gzo ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags sdig pa 'tshal ba rnams kyi slad du ma lags
5a5(sna tshogs): sdig pa spyod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul khrims nyams pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul khrims yongs su ma dag pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ lta ba nyams pa rnams//
5a6(sna tshogs): kyi slad du ma lags bdud kyi spyod yul la spyod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ bdag la bstod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ gzhan la smod pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags//
5a7(sna tshogs): rnyed pa dang bkur sti la gdu ba rnams kyi srang du ma lags/ lhung bzed dang chos gos la chags pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ tshul 'chos pa rnams kyi slad du ma lags/
5b1(sna tshogs): gsag can rnams kyi slad du ma lags/ gzhogs yongs can rnams kyi srang du ma lags/ rdzob kyipa 'angal rnams kyi srung du ma lags/ rnyed pa la rnyed par dru 'dus kyi
5b2(sna tshogs): slang du ma 'gas/ bco pa ldan 'das sems can de la na rnams sa srung du/ 'dos de bzhin ga shegs pa la thab ma lags so// bcom ldan pangs ses nga blangs byang
5b3(sna tshogs): mabyed de'i ye shes tshol ba dang / chags pa ma mchis pa'i ye shes dang / rang byung gi mi shes dang / mi mnyam pa dang mnyam pa'i ye shes deng / bla na med pa'i ye shes tshos pa de ngo
5b4(sna tshogs): dang / gang dag bdag dang pha rol kyang ma dmigs na/ bdag la bstod pa dang bzhin la spong pa lta ga la mchi ste/ bcom ldan 'das ra bcad pa lta du rang rgyal ma mchis pa/ drun
5b5(sna tshogs): rngu byung ba/ gdol bu lta bur sems dman pa/ sems sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung dang / nam mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sas
5b6(sna tshogs): dnga'i chen po rnams kyi slad du bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das gang dag chos kyang mi dmigs shing / rlom sems su mi bgyid la/ mngon par
5b7(sna tshogs): zhen pa ma mchis na/ chos ma lags pa lta ga la mchis te byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi slad du/ bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom
6a1(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bsam pa dag pa g.yo ma mchis pa/ sgyu ma mchis pa/ drang ba/ sems mnyam pa/ sems can thams cad la sbran pa dang
6a2(sna tshogs): snying brtse ba can yang dag par 'dzin du stsol ba/ yang dag par gzengs bstod pa yang dag par dga' bar bgyid pa/ khur chen po khyer ba/ theg pa chen po la mngon par zhugs pa/
6a3(sna tshogs): bgyi ba chen pos so sor nye bar gnas pa/ snying rje chen po dang ldan pa/ sems can thams cang bde ba thob par bgyid pa/ 'dren po/ rnam par 'dren pa/ yongs su 'dren pa
6a4(sna tshogs): chos thams cad la mi rten par gnas pa skye ba'i gnas thams cad mi tshol ba bdud kyi zhags pa thams cad las rnam par grol ba 'dun pa can/ brtson 'grus dang ldan
6a5(sna tshogs): pa/ bag mchis pa/ chos thams cad kyi dam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa/ the tshom thams cad gcod pa la mkhas pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
6a6(sna tshogs): chen po rnams kyi slad du/ bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das sems can gang dag sangs rgyas kyi ye shes la'ang rlom sems su
6a7(sna tshogs): mi bgyid cing / mngon par mi zhen la/ chags par mi gnas shing / rlom sems thams cad las yang dag par 'das pa'i lam la gnas par lam du zhugs pa/ lam
6b1(sna tshogs): stospong pa'i sems can rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag gi slad du/ bcom ldan 'das bdag de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom
6b2(sna tshogs): ldan 'das bdag ni sems can thams cad la bde ba dang / lhag na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang / bla na ma mchis pa'i bde ba dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i bde ba dang / sangs
6b3(sna tshogs): rjes ky-i bde ba dang / 'dus ma bgyis pa'i bde banye bar bsgrub par 'tshal te/ bdag sems can thams cad kyi don drung / snyan pa dang / bde ba dang / grub pa dang /
6b4(sna tshogs): blang ba'i slad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa la zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das bdag ni the tshom ma mchis par 'dzul zhing / the tshom mchis nas kyang / sems can rnams kyi
6b5(sna tshogs): cho ma rang tu spong ba'i slad du/ chos bshad par 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das bdag sems can thams cad kyi the tsom bsal ba'i slad du/ bcom ldan 'das la zhu
6b6(sna tshogs): lags so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das sems can thams cad ni sdug bsngal drang po mthun zhing / rnye pa 'tsham la/ sems can thams cad ni bde ba do du/
6b7(sna tshogs): / ldan 'das shes riri ma gtogs par/ gzhan po me khyen rnams kyi ba gang yang bdag gis pa yang zhing / ma ldan 'das kyang ma
7a1(sna tshogs): dpa'i theg pa/ theg pa chen po ma gtogs par/ sems can rnams kyi bde ba gang yang ma mchis te/ bcom ldan 'das bdag gis dor gyi dbang 'dir thong bas/
7a2(sna tshogs): sems can rnams la bde ba nye bar bsgrub pa'i slad du/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhu lags so// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi don 'di yang dag par mthong
7a3(sna tshogs): bas/ bdag gis de bzhin gshegs pa la ngor 'di zhu lags so// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po
7a4(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnams par gnon pa la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gdon pa legs so legs so// khyod skye bo phal po che la snying brtse ba'i phyir/ de bzhin
7a5(sna tshogs): gshegs pa la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di 'dri ba ni khyod kyi yon tan gyi mtha' gtogs par sla ba ma yin no// de'i phyir rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa legs par nyon la rab tu yid la
7a6(sna tshogs): zung zhig dang / ngas khyod la bshad do// bcom ldan 'das legs so zhes gsol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ bcom ldan 'das
7a7(sna tshogs): kyi ltar nyar pa dang / bcom ldan 'das kyis de skad ces bka' stsal to// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa khyod 'di skad du/ bcom ldan 'das khyod shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa shes rang /
7b1(sna tshogs): kyi rol tu phyir pa zhes dbyi ba bcom ldan 'das rdzatsam myopar byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhesang kyishes ra ni/ rludus na 'grus mang sa/
7b2(sna tshogs): ba shes rab kyi pha rol tu dran pa ni/ tshes gang gis kyang rjod par bye bas smim/ sa rab pa ral tu phyin pa / tshig rnams su ltas 'dus pas+ho/ la
7b3(sna tshogs): par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni/ 'di shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// 'jis shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o// de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'o zhes/
7b4(sna tshogs): brjod par mi nus so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di chos thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yin te/ de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal
7b5(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnor pa/ shes rab nyid kyang de bzhin gshegs pas ma rnyed ma dmigs na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ljang dmigs par ga la 'gyur/ rab kyi rdul gyis rnam
7b6(sna tshogs): nga/ shes 'a chos pa na shes pan chos bams ca pa sa rji sa / ra sa
7b7(sna tshogs): bag mam thams cad gu tu rig pag pa na che mo 'di dag thams cad ni rnam pa gzhanan/ chos thams cad rnam pa pozhan du brjod / chos thams cad ni rjod pa las
8a1(sna tshogs): rnam par grol ba ma yin no// gang chos thams cad kun tu shes pa dang / gang chos thams cad kun tu rig pa de'ang tshig gis brjod par mi rus mod kyi/ 'od kyang ji
8a2(sna tshogs): ltar sems can rnams kyis shes par gyur pa de ltar shes rab ces bya'o// 'di ni btags pa zhes bya ste/ de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
8a3(sna tshogs): chos thams cad ni gdags su med/ gzung du med/ bshad du med/ snang ba med de/ de lta bur kun tu rig pa re ni kun tu rig pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnond pa
8a4(sna tshogs): shes rab ces bya ba de ni shes pa'ang ma yid/ kun tu mi shes pa'ang ma yin/ de las kyang ma yin/ de las ma yin pa'ang ma yin te/ de'i phyir shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal
8a5(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnod pa/ de ni mi shes pa'i spyod yul yang ma yin/ ye shes kyi spyod yul yang ma yin/ bri shes pa'i yul yang ma yin/ ye shes kyi yul yang ma yin te/
8a6(sna tshogs): ye shes ni yul meng ba'o// gal te ye shes la yul yod du zin na mi shes par 'gyur ro// ye shes ni mi shes pa las ma yin/ mi shes pa'ang ye shes las ma yin/
8a7(sna tshogs): shes ri mi shes pa ma yin mi shes pa'ang ye shes ma yin te/ ye shes kyis ye shes shes bya'o// ye shes kyis mi shes pa zhes mi bya'o// mi shes pas ye shes shes
8b1(sna tshogs): bu'o/ de la ye shes ni 'di'o// ye shes de ni 'di'i 'o// ye shes de ni 'das so// ye shes de ni 'di'i phyir ro zhes ye shes cung zad sdang bstan par mi nus te/ de'i
8b2(sna tshogs): phyir ye shes de ni ye shes nyid kyis med do// ye shes kyang ye shes su mi gnas te/ mi shes pas kyang ye shes shes mibya'o// ga rje mi shes pa ye shes shes d+ha na nA~M/
8b3(sna tshogs): phyir byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyang ye shes can du 'gyur ro// gang ye shes dang mi shes pa mi dmigs shing / ye shes dang mi shes pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongs
8b4(sna tshogs): su shes pa de nyid ye shes shes bya ste/ ye shes ni ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du ma yin no// de bas na ye shes ni brjod par bya ba ma yin zhing yul thams cad lus rab tu
8b5(sna tshogs): 'das pa ste/ ye shes ni gang gi yul yang ma yin no// ye shes kyi yul yang gang yang ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ ye shes bstan pa'i yul yang
8b6(sna tshogs): ma yid/ phyogs kyang ma yin pa 'di gang gis shes pa de ni ye shes can nam/ ye shes can ma yin pa zhes bya ba'i grangs su mi 'gro'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/
8b7(sna tshogs): gang 'di ltar rab tu shes pa dang / rjes su rtogs pa dang / kun tu shes pa de ni shes rab ces bya'o// rab kyi rgyal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang 'di ltar mngon par gas
9a1(sna tshogs): pa mngon sum du byed pa de ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab rjes bya'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no//
9a2(sna tshogs): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'jig rjen nyid kyang ming rigs na/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab lta ga la yod de/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab kyis/ gang 'jig rten
9a3(sna tshogs): las sgrol bar 'gyur ba lta ci smos/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ des 'dzag rten mi dmigs pas/ ci'ang sgrol bar mi byed de/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces bya'o//
9a4(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'jig rten zhes bya ba 'di ni brtags pa zhes brjod pa ste/ btags pa ni 'jig rten las yang dag par 'das pa ma yin gyi/ btags pa thams
9a5(sna tshogs): cad las yang dag par 'das pa ni 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o// 'da' bar bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa ma yin gyi'ada' bar mi bya ba ni 'jig rten las 'das pa'o//
9a6(sna tshogs): de ci'i phyir zhe ra/ de la gang 'da' bar bya ba dang / gang gis 'da' bar bya ba'i chos phra rab tsam yang med pas/ de'i phyir 'das pa zhes bya ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa la ni 'jig
9a7(sna tshogs): rten yang med/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'ang med do// bla na med pa la ni bsgral ba med de/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gdon pa 'di
9b1(sna tshogs): na 'jis rte las 'das pa'i shes rabya brtan pa skyes bya ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces de sang du brjod pa ba'i duni ma yin no// de ba'i phyi na/ ga //
9b2(sna tshogs): las 'das pa ri brjod par bya ba ma yin gyi/ de ni brgal ba ste/ de la ni 'da' bar bya ba ci'ang med pas/ de'i phyir 'jig rten las 'das pa'i shes rab ces pa'o// rab kyi tshul
9b3(sna tshogs): gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de la gang nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab des ci nges par rtogs/ 'di la ni nges par rtogs par bya ba ci'ang med do// gal te nge nges par rtogs par bya
9b4(sna tshogs): 'ga' zhig yod du zin na ni/ 'di shes rab kyis nges par rtogs pa zhes gangadags na/ gang gis kyang mi rtogs shing kun rtogs pa ma yin la/ kun rtogs par 'gyur ba'i
9b5(sna tshogs): bye brag gang yang mi dmigs so// nges par rtogs zhes bya ba ni kra 'di la rtogs par byed pa ci'ang med cing / kun tu rdzogs par bya ba'ang med de/ de la rtogs par byed pa ci'ang med
9b6(sna tshogs): cing kun tu rtogs par bya ba'ang med pas/ de'i phyir nges par rtogs pa zhes bya'o// 'di la ri gang yang mthar 'gro ba med cing dbus su'ang ma yin te/ de'i phyir nges
9b7(sna tshogs): bar rtogs pa zhes bya'o// nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis rtogs pa ni steng ma rtogs te/ gang du'ang mi rgyug/ rnam par mi rgyug/ kun tu mi chug ste/ de'i phyir nges
10a1(sna tshogs): par rtogs pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ nges par rtogs shes bya ba'i shes rab kyis/ ci nges par rtogs she na gang ci snang ba de thams
10a2(sna tshogs): cad nges par rtogs so// gang gis nges par rtogs she na/ shes rab kyis so// shes rab kyis ji ltar nges par rtogs she na/ gang btags pa'i mtshan nyid de thams cad mtshan
10a3(sna tshogs): nying meng pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa'ang btags pa'i mtshan nyid du'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang 'di lta bu'i shes rab dang ldan pas nges par rtogs pa des ni/
10a4(sna tshogs): khams gsum rtogs so// ji ltar rtogs she na/ khams gsum ni khams med par rtogs te/ 'di la ni khams rtogs pa ci'ang med do// des khams gsum ni khams med par
10a5(sna tshogs): rtogs so// gang de ltar khams gsum khams med par nges par rtogs pa dang / gang gis de ltar khams gsum nges par rtogs pa de ni// nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan
10a6(sna tshogs): pa zhes bya'o// ji ltar na nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan zhe na/ nges par rtogs par bya ba ni/ mi dge ba gang yang med de/ de thams cad dag par nges par rtogs te
10a7(sna tshogs): de nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis rab tu 'dab 'o// de de ltar rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan pas gang ci mthong ba dang / thos pa dang / mnams pa dang / myangs pa dang /
10b1(sna tshogs): rig padadu/ rnam par shes pa de dag thams cad nges par rtogs so// ji ltar dar rtogs shen/ mi rtag / sprus bsngal ba da / 'bras dang/ nad drung / zu
10b2(sna tshogs): dang stong pa nyid dang sdig pa dang / gnod pa dang / mtha' ma dang / 'jig pa dang / 'jig pa'i chos nyid dang g.yo ba dang / 'jig pa'i tshul ca
10b3(sna tshogs): bdag med pa dang / mi skye ba dang / mi 'gog pa dang / mtshan nyid med par te/ rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnod pa/ de ni bsil bar gyur padrug rngu med pa zhes bya'o//
10b4(sna tshogs): rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnod pa/ 'di lta ste/ dper na zug rngu med pa zhes bya ba'i slar gyi rigs de gang na 'dug pa de ni drug rngu thams cing sel cing nges par 'don to//
10b5(sna tshogs): bzhin du 'di lta bu'i chos rnams dang ldan pa'i dge slong ni drug rngu med cing bsil bar gyur la/ nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab dang ldan zhing drug med la rtag tu gnas la/ nges par
10b6(sna tshogs): rtogs pa'i shes rab gyis khams gsupa thams cad la mi chags shing bdud kyi zhigs pa thams cad las rab tu 'angs so// rab kyi rtul gyis rnam par gdor pa/ 'di lta
10b7(sna tshogs): dper rdo rje ni drug pa'i phyi gang du bcugs pa de dang de nyid du nges pa'i phigs so// de bzhin du dge slong gos nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab kyis yongs su yin par rngo
11a1(sna tshogs): lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gang du btsugs pa dang / gang du spyod pa de dag thams cad nges par rtogs so// de nges par rtogs pa'i shes rab 'jig rten las 'das
11a2(sna tshogs): pa yang dag par sdug bsngal zad par 'gyur ba dang ldan pas/ chags pa med pa ni gsum rig pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa rig pa zhes bya ba de ni ma
11a3(sna tshogs): rig pa nye bar zhi ba'i tshig bla dgas so// ma rig pa yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba de ni sdug bsngal gyi phung po nye bar zhi ba'i tshig bla dgas so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod
11a4(sna tshogs): pa 'di lta ste/ dper na sman pa mkhas pa gsal ba yid rdo ba/ lhag par rtog pa dang ldan pa sman thams cad la mkhras pa/ rAd ldang ba thams cad
11a5(sna tshogs): la mkhas pa/ sdug bsngal thams cad las rnam par 'grel pa des nad pa gang dang gang la gso ba byas pa de dang de 'tshe'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar de slar thams
11a6(sna tshogs): cad la mkhas shing / nang ldang ba thams cad la mkhas te/ nad thams cad las thar par byed pa'i phyir ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de bzhin du rig pa gsum
11a7(sna tshogs): bos ni ma rig pa thams cad nye b.rare zhi bar 'gyur/ sdug bsngal thams cad 'joms par 'gyur/ rga shi dang / mya ngan dang / smre sngags 'don pa dang / sdug bsngal
11b1(sna tshogs): bdang / yid mi bded dang / bzlag pa thams cad bye pa'i bar gyu / rang kyin la sa rnam par gnon pa/ de ni 'dig rna rnams 'das pa shes pa sa
11b2(sna tshogs): du'o/ mas kyis rnam pa rdzun du/ ngas 'di las dpo smranas/ rmed par skye ba mang+yas da dUrA/ sa sa bya
11b3(sna tshogs): rtogs par 'gro bdi/ 'jig rten na no shes rang mchog/ ces bshar ro// rab kyi phul gyis rnam par gnon pa/ skyed par skye ba yongs su zad pa zhes bya ba krung gi tshig zu
11b4(sna tshogs): yin zhen/ deni 'byung ba dang rlab par btu rdzogs pa'i tshig bladags so// 'byung ba dang chub pa ga bzhin// kun 'byung ba'i chos stong rung ste/ de babs rtsod ni 'gaklu 'i tshe
11b5(sna tshogs): 'di ltar kur 'byung ba dang nub pa rab tu rdzogs so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ kun 'byung ba zhes bya ba de ni 'byung ba'i tshig bla dgas so// nub pa zhes bya ba de ni 'gog pa'i
11b6(sna tshogs): tshig bla dgas te/ 'byung ba dang nub pa zhes ji skad du brjod pa de bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ kun 'byung ba gang ci 'angadra rung ste/ de ni kur 'byung ba'i chos
11b7(sna tshogs): ma yin no// rab kyi rgyal gyis rdib par gnod pa mnyam pa las 'byung ba gang yang med de/ de ni kur 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro// de mnyam pa nyid kyi rjes su song ste/ de'i phyir kur/
12a1(sna tshogs): 'byung ba zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa / mnyam pa'i rjes su song ba zhes bya ba ni/ 'di la 'byung ba gang yang rnyed de/ kun 'byung bar yang mi 'gyur
12a2(sna tshogs): ro// de'i rang bzhin gang yin pa de ni/ rang gi ngang gis 'jig cing de ni 'gog pa ste/ de la ni 'gog pa gang yang med do// mnyam pa ni bla na med pa'i 'gog pa ste/ gang la skye
12a3(sna tshogs): ba med pa de la 'gog pa med de/ de ni 'gog pa'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ltar skye ba med cing 'gog pa med pa'i phyir gang 'byung ba dang nub pa rtogs pa de nub pa rab tu
12a4(sna tshogs): rtogs pa ste/ de'i phyir 'byung ba dang nub pa rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ rab tu rtogs shes bya ba de ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yongs su shes
12a5(sna tshogs): pa zhes bya'o// gang brten nas chos gang skye ba de nyidi la brten nas chos de med de/ 'di ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba rab tu rtogs pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa
12a6(sna tshogs): ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i yang dag pa nyid ji lta ba bzhin du skye ba med par bstan to// mi skye ba ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba ste/ mi 'byung ba mnyam pas/ de'i phyir rten cing
12a7(sna tshogs): 'brel par 'byung ba zhes bya'o// gang skye ba med pa de la 'gog po ga la yod de/ bgog pa dang mi 'gal ba de ni rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i 'gog pa med pa ste/ skye ba med pa de ni rten
12b1(sna tshogs): cing 'brel bar 'byung ba zhes bya'o// gang 'brel par 'byung ba de ni ma byung ba'o// gang mabyung ba de ni 'das pa ma yin/ ma 'ongs pa ma yin/ da ltar byung ba ma yinan/ gang 'dus pa
12b2(sna tshogs): pa yin/ ma 'ongs pa ma yin/ da ltar byung ba ma yin pa de la 'gag pa med do// gang la 'gog pa reng bu de ri blo skye ba shes pa zhes bya'o// glang gis mi skye bar shes pa de da la
12b3(sna tshogs): skyeng ba ma yin/ 'grog pa mngod sum du byed de'ang ma yid no// gang mi skyed pa de 'gog par bri byed de/ skye ba yid re ri 'gog par yang shes so// grang mo skyed pa des chos thams
12b4(sna tshogs): tsong 'gog pa nyid du shes shing mthong la/ rab tu rtogs shing mngon sum du byas te/ de'i phyir 'gog pa mngon sum du byas pa zhes bya'o// zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi
12b5(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa mi shes pa zang pa de'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// gang gis zad ce na/ mi zad pos zad de/ de'i zad pa'ang mi mthong ngo // rab kyi rtsal gyis
12b6(sna tshogs): rnam par gnon pa/ bri shes pa med pas/ de'i phyir de zad pa shes pa zhes du'o// rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnod pa/ mi shes pa yongs su shes pa de'i phyir mi shes pa
12b7(sna tshogs): zad de zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// mi shes pa ni bod pa'am/ ma zad pa ma yin te/ 'di ni shes pa dang bral ba'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par/
13a1(sna tshogs): gnod pa 'di ri yang dag pa'i lta ba bzhin du yongs su shes pa ste/ de'i dri'i bral ba zhes bya'o// mi shes pa dang bral ba dang / shes pa dang bral
13a2(sna tshogs): ba'adi las gzhan ci'ang mi dmigs so// ye shes nyid kyang mi dmigs na/ gang zad pa las rnam par grol ba mi shes pa lnga ci smos te/ de'i phyir zad pa shes pa zhes bya'o//
13a3(sna tshogs): ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin no// zad pa gang yin pa de la tha snyad du gdags pa gang yang med mod kyi/ 'on kyang 'di ltar ri shes pa zad pa dang / zad pa shes pa zhes
13a4(sna tshogs): bster to// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ gang gis chos thams cad mi zad pa dang / zad pa shes pa la brtag pa khong du chud pa de zad pa shes pa dang bral te/ zad
13a5(sna tshogs): pa med pa'i mtha' rjes su thob bo// mtha' med pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// chos thams cad ni mya ngan las 'das
13a6(sna tshogs): pa'i mtha' ste/ mtha' med pa'o// mtha' thams cad chud pa ni mya ngan las 'das pa'i mtha' zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// mya ngan las 'das
13a7(sna tshogs): pa ni tha snyad thams cad chad pa brjod par bya ba ma yin pa ste/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gdon pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings bstan pa 'di'ang ji skad du bstan pa/
13b1(sna tshogs): ba'i dun pa yin no// kun thamams cad las yang dag par 'dus bya sa/ myang na las 'dus pa'i dbyings kyi ska du med de/ byud pa thams ra rung tu dang bde
13b2(sna tshogs): byung nga las 'das pa'i dbying sa shes bya'o// mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings thos bya ba gang yin pa de / 'jig ce las 'das pa shes rab dres par rnags pa
13b3(sna tshogs): bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ mya ngan la 'das pa'i dbyings de ni yul na mi gnas/ phyogs na mi gnas pa zhes bstan to// rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon
13b4(sna tshogs): pa de la shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang zhe na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnor pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la tshu rol lar/ pha rol gang yang rnyed do// 8
13b5(sna tshogs): kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gal te shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa la tshu rol la ru pha rol dmigasun ni dri bzhin gshegs pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshu rol 'am
13b6(sna tshogs): pha rol shad pa zhig na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshu rol mi dmigs pas/ de'i phyir rob pha rol kyang med mod kyi/ 'o
13b7(sna tshogs): kyang rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba de ni chos thams cad kyi pha rol lo// de'i phyir shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ste/ ji skad
14a1(sna tshogs): du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni tshig dang las kyis nye bar gnas pa ma yin te/ she
14a2(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni bstan du med pa'o// chos thams cad de ltar khong du chud na/ de ni ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud de mi 'gal lo// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de la khong du chud pa
14a3(sna tshogs): TI'ang med cing / rab tu rtogs pa'ang med pa'i phyir ro// khong du chud pa dang / rab tu rtogs pa mnyam pa nyid ni byang chub ste/ chos thams cad khong du chud pa ni byang chub cis bya'o//
14a4(sna tshogs): ji ltar chos thams cad khong du chud ce na/ 'di la byang chub gang yang med/ 'di khong du chud pa gang yang med do/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab kyi rdzal gyis rnam par gnod pa
14a5(sna tshogs): gal te byang chub dmigs na ni/ byang chub la'ang byang chub dmigs par 'gyur ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa / byang chub la ni byang chub med de/ de ltar byang chub 'di
14a6(sna tshogs): mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o// khong du chud pa med pa dang / rab tu rtogs pa med pas rjes su rdzogs pa zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjed pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// chos
14a7(sna tshogs): thams cad ni khong du chung ba ma yin/ rab tu rtogs pa ma yin te/ chos ni chos kyi ngo bo nyid kyis med do// de ltar khong du chud ba de ni byang chub ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnab par
14b1(sna tshogs): gdod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub ma migs shing / de bzhin ga shegs pas ni byang chub rnam par ma g+sa ste/ rlung chu ni rnam par rig par du ba cwa yin/ rA
14b2(sna tshogs): rnam par rig par bya ba ma yin no// de bzhin gshegs pas ni byang chub ma mkhyen ma bskyed de/ byang chub ni ma skyes shing mngon par mi nub bo// zung drung na su'i yang sa yi 'omi/
14b3(sna tshogs): byang chub las bas can nam/ sems can du gdags pa gang yang med do// gang lo sems can nam/ sems can du gdags pa med pa de la 'dri byang chub sems dpa'
14b4(sna tshogs): 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes ji ltar brjod/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ byang chub la byang chub kyang myod byang chub la sems can
14b5(sna tshogs): yang med de/ byang chub 'di ni shin tu 'das pa'o// byang chub 'di ni ma skyes pa'o// byang chub 'di ni mngon par ma grub pa'i// byang chub 'di ni mtshan nyid med pa ste/ 'di
14b6(sna tshogs): la sems can phreng cing mo dmigs so// byang chub ni sems can gyis btags pa ma yin gyi/ sems can med par khong du chud pa ni byang chub ces bya'o// byang chub sems can ma
14b7(sna tshogs): yid par gang gis shes pa de byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can gyi 'du shes
15a1(sna tshogs): kyis bskyed pa ma yin gyi/ sems can gyi 'du shes rnam par 'jig pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin
15a2(sna tshogs): ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni brjod par bya ma yin zhing byang chub sems dpa' ni sems can gyi rang bzhin dang bral ba'i phyir ro// byang chub ni sems cad
15a3(sna tshogs): du 'du shes pa dang bral ba ste/ gang gis byang chub de ltar shes pa byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// byang chub ji lta bur shes she na/ byang chub 'di ni shin tu 'dres pa'o// byang
15a4(sna tshogs): chub 'di ri bye ba ma yin pa'o// byang chub 'di ni skye ba med pa 'gog pa med pa'o// byang chub ni byang chub kyis shes par mi byed/ byang chub ni rnam par shes par bya ba ma yin
15a5(sna tshogs): rnam par rig par bya ba ma yin/ gdags par bya ba ma yin te/ mngon par ma grub pa ni byang chub ces bya'o// rnam par mi rtog pa dang / rtog pa bcad pa'i phyir/ gang gis
15a6(sna tshogs): khong du chud ba dag rab tu rtogs pa de'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ste/ 'di skad du brjod pa bzhin du ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can med pa'i phyir ro//
15a7(sna tshogs): gal te byang chub sems dpa' yang dag par dmigs na ni/ 'di ni byang chub 'di ni sems can zhes byang chub de'ang rnyed par 'gyur ro// sems can med pa dang / sems
15b1(sna tshogs): na paban pa dang / mas can dadu dusu par 'ang du rung pan byung dru ba sems dpa' zhes bya'o// sems ldan med dang smras pa du 'a sa rnam par smra/
15b2(sna tshogs): chub sams dpa' zhes byag/ de nini phyir rnyer/ sems can gyi sa shes ma bdi de/ sems cad med pa'i myig bla rags so// sems cad kyi 'das me pa'i phyir
15b3(sna tshogs): sems can la sems can med do// gal te sems can la sems cad yod na ni/ sems can gyi khams shes mi b+he'o// sems can gyi khams shes bya ba de ni/ 'angs med
15b4(sna tshogs): par bstan te/ 'ams med pa ni sems can gyi khams so// gal te sems can gyi khams sems can gyi khams su gyur na ni/ srog de lus de yin par 'gyur ro// ci ste sems
15b5(sna tshogs): can gyi khams rnam par grol ba khams gsum du gyur na ni srog kyang gzhan/ lus kyang gzhan du 'gyur ro// khams med pa ni sems can gyi khams te/ brdas tha snyad du gdags
15b6(sna tshogs): pa'i tshig tu 'gro'o// sems can gyi khams la ni khams med de/ khams ma rtogs pas sems can gyi khams med do// chos thams cad ri khams med pa ste/ ngas de la dgongs
15b7(sna tshogs): nas sems car gyi khams ni gang ba'am dri bar yang mi mngon no zhes bshad do// de ci'i phyir 'or/ sems cad gyi lams rab tu ben pa'i phyir/ sems cad gyi 'ang ni
16a1(sna tshogs): sems can ma yin no// ji ltar sems can mi khams bri ba dang gang bar mi mngon pa bzhin du/ chos thangs cad kyang driba'ang/ bang bar mi rjod/
16a2(sna tshogs): gang dag dri ba'am/ gang bar 'gyur bar chos thams cad la yongs su grub pa gang yang med de/ gang gis de ltar rjes thams cad khong du chung ba de ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos 'o
16a3(sna tshogs): chud pa zhes bya ste/ ngas 'di la dgongs nas/ ji ltar sems can gyi khams bri ba 'am/ glang bar mi mngon pa de bzhin du/ chos thams cad kyang bri ba 'ab/ gang bar mi ring
16a4(sna tshogs): ro zhes bya ba bshad do// gang yang yongs su ma grub pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad byi ba ma yin/ gang bu ma yin pa des/ sangs rgyas kyis chos kyang bri ba ma yid/ grang ba
16a5(sna tshogs): ma yin no// de ltar chos thams cad khong du chud pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams bri ba med cing / gang ba med pa'o// chos thams cad bri ba med cing du/ gdu ba med du/
16a6(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas kyi chos shes bya ba de ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshig bla dgas ma yin no// sangs rgyas kyi chos ni gang gis kyang bri ba 'am/ gang bar bya bar mi nus so// de ra
16a7(sna tshogs): shen/ 'din chos thams cad 'ong du chung ba'i phyir te/ gang chos thams cad 'ong du chung ba de la bri ba 'am/ gang ba'i chos ci'ang med do// chos thams cad ces bya ba ni chos kyi
16b1(sna tshogs): dbyings kyi chog tha dag / chos kyi dbyings la b+hA ba 'am/ gang bu med do// de ci'i phyir te na/ chos kyi dbyings ni mtha' yas pa'i phyir ro// sems car gyi khabs dang rdo bya/
16b2(sna tshogs): dbyings ni tha dad du mi dmigs so// sems can gyi khams dang chos kyi dbyings bri ba 'am/ gang ba nga migs pa'am/ yod pa ma yin ti/ gang gis de ltar khong du chud pa de
16b3(sna tshogs): chub ces bya'o// de'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams bri ba 'am/ gang bar mi mngon zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ bri ba med cing / gang ba med pa zhes ji skad
16b4(sna tshogs): du smra ba de ni/ brtag pa yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthong ba'i tshig bla dgas so// de la ni ci'ang bsal ba 'am/ gzhag par mi nus te/ gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang
16b5(sna tshogs): chub ces bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa byang chub ces bya ba de ni sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid do// sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid ji lta bu zhe na/ chos thams cad kyi mtshar
16b6(sna tshogs): nyid mtshan nyid med pa de ni sangs rgyas kyi mtshan nyid do// byang chub ni mtshan nyid med pa ste/ mtshan nyid kyi rang bzhin las bzlog pa'o// gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang
16b7(sna tshogs): chub ces bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ni chos thams cad rjes su rtogs pas/ byang chub sems dpa'
17a1(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnams par gnon pa/ gang la la zhig chos 'di rab tu mi shes khong du ma chud par/ bdag byang chub sems dpa'
17a2(sna tshogs): zhes khas 'chen/ de ni byang chub sems dpa'i sa las ring ngo // de ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams las ring ngo // de ni byang chub sems dpa'i ming gis lha dang mi dang
17a3(sna tshogs): lha ma yin dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten la bslu ba'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ byang chub sems dpar gyur na ni/ de'i phyir sems can thams cad kyang byang chub
17a4(sna tshogs): sems dpar 'gyur ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i sa zhes bya ba de ni tshig gi las tsam ma yin no// tshig gis bla ra med pa yang
17a5(sna tshogs): dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar rus so// tshig gi las kyis byang chub dang / byang chub sems dpa'i chos rnams thob par mi 'gyur ro// rab
17a6(sna tshogs): kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa sems can thams cad ni byang chub la spyod mod kyi/ mi shes shing khong du ma chung de/ de'i phyir de dag byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya'o//
17a7(sna tshogs): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ sems can rnams sems can med par mi shes pa'i phyir ro// gal te de ltar shes na bdag gis sbyong pa dag gis/ byang chub sems dpa' dag tu 'gyur ba'i
17b1(sna tshogs): rigs so// sems can thams cad dbyin du logyi pas rang gi spyod pa dang / rang kri sus dang / rang gi spyong stsal ba tu myigs s+ho/ gas te rang kyi sbyod pa
17b2(sna tshogs): ni de dgu sar gang la'ang rnam par cig cing spyad par gyu ro// rnam par rdzog pa dang spyod pa de dag gis skyes pa sa mi'i skye ba mams cad yang dbu ni yin pa
17b3(sna tshogs): shing snod kyang / de dag byang chub la dmigs paM snyam du rlom sems su byed de/ dmigs pa'i spyod cing / rtog pa la spyod pa de dag la byang chub ga la yod/ byang chub sems
17b4(sna tshogs): dpa'i chos rnams ga la yod/ gang gis chos de lta bur rab tu shes pa de dag slar yang dag pa ma yon pa'i dmigs pa la mo spyod cing de dag ni phyir chos gang srung rlom sems
17b5(sna tshogs): su mi byed de/ de'i phyir spyod pa med pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' ni rtog pa dang rnam par rtog pa la mi spyod do// gang la rtog pa med pa
17b6(sna tshogs): de la spyod pa gang yang med do// gang la rnam par rtog pa med pa de la stong pa'i don gang yang med do// sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa thams cad ni rnam par
17b7(sna tshogs): mi rtog par spyod cing thams cad rlom sems med la/ dmigs pa dang bcas pa ma yin pa ste/ chos thams cad de ltar rab tu shes pa de ni/ phyir dmigs pa 'am/ rnam
18a1(sna tshogs): par rtog pa la spyod pa 'am/ rnam par spyod pa med de/ de ni spyod pa med pa'i tshul gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod pa zhes bya'o// rab tu
18a2(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ltar na byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la spyod pa yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ grong de ltar chos 'ong
18a3(sna tshogs): du chud cing rab tu rtogs pa de'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// des sems can du 'du shes bsal bas/ sems can med pa zhes bya ba de ni/ byang chub sems
18a4(sna tshogs): dpa'i tshig bla dgas so// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ nges sems can thams cad yang dag pa ma yin pa dang / sems can thams cad sems can ma yir pa dang / sems can thams
18a5(sna tshogs): cad ni phyin ci log gi sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni yongs su brtags pas sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni yod pa ma yin pa la dmigs pas sems cad dang //
18a6(sna tshogs): sems cad thams cad ri rang gis spyod pa rnam par ma rung bar byas pas sems can dang / sems can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can no zhes shes pa'i phyir ro// de ci'i
18a7(sna tshogs): phyir zhe na/ sems car thams cad ni chos gang dag med pa'i chos de dag mngon par 'du byed pas/ de'i phyir sems can thams cad ni ma rig pa 'du byed pas sems can zhes bya'o//

18b2(sna tshogs): dun rgyur ma sa mas ca dang shA rdza kyi smras par gan pa 'di ltar du sa
18b3(sna tshogs): byi ma na nga sa na / sa nga 'du sa drug+sa sa su
18b4(sna tshogs): zhe'am/ ngab zhe'am/ ra'o zhes bya ba sa sems can zhes bu da'i chos gang yang med de/ gang gi byor red pa de'i phyir sems can ni nang dug pa ma yid pa zhes du'o// gang dag pa pa me pa
18b5(sna tshogs): zhes bya ba de ni sems cad med pa'i tshig bla dgas so// de ltar sems can du 'du shes pa yang dag pa ma yin pa la mngon par zhen pa de ltar sems can rnams yang dag pa ma yin pa las
18b6(sna tshogs): bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya ba de la ni yang dag pa ci'ang med cing ma byung du'o// chos thams cad kyang yang dag bla ma yin zhing ma byung
18b7(sna tshogs): ba'o// de la sems can yang dag pa ma yin pa la lhag par chags pa de ni rnam par 'ching ba ste/ de'i phyir yang dag pa mi yin pa la dmigs pa ni sems can zhes bya'o// de dag ni spyod pa
19a1(sna tshogs): gang khong du chud pas/ byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba'i rang gi spyod pa de mi shes te/ yongs su ma rtogs pas sems can ni yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o//
19a2(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ gang de ltar khong du chud pa de ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya ba de ni/ gang gis chos thams cad khong du chud cing
19a3(sna tshogs): shes la sems can rjes su rtogs pa'i tshig bla dgas so// ji ltar shes she na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa dang / ma byung ba dang / phyin ci log ma yin par ro// ji ltar byis pa so
19a4(sna tshogs): so'i skye bo dag gis brtags pa de dag ni de bzhin du ma yin no// ji ltar byis pa so so'i skye bo dag gis rnyed pa de dag de bzhin du ma yin te/ de'i phyir byang chub sems dpa' zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir/
19a5(sna tshogs): zhe na/ byang chub ni ma brtags rnam par brtags shing byang chub mngon par ma bsgrubs la/ mi dmigs pa'i phyir ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa de bzhin gshegs pas
19a6(sna tshogs): byang chub ma brnyes so// chos thams cad mi rnyed cing / chos thams cad mi dmigs pa'i phyir byang chub ces bya'o// de lta bu ni sangs rgyas kyi byang chub ces bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa
19a7(sna tshogs): bzhin du ni ma yin no// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa gang dag byang chub kyi phyir sems 'di bskyed par bya'o// zhes byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / gang du bdag gis sems//
19b1(sna tshogs): dasteng par bya ba'i byang dru yod do// zhes byung chu rlom sems su byed pa de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' zhes mi bya ste/ de gni sems pa na skyes pa zhes na'o// duba'i
19b2(sna tshogs): na/ 'di ltar de dag ni skye bar mngon par 'on cid / sems su mngon par zher nas/ byang chub la mngon pa zhen pa'i phyir ro/ gang dag byang chub kyi byor sems bskyed par dag do
19b3(sna tshogs): byang chub kyi sems la mngon par zhen pa zhes bya'o// gang gi phyir mngon par 'du byed pa de'i phyir/ byang chub tu sems skyed de/ de bas na mngon par 'du byed pa ni sems can zhes bya ste/
19b4(sna tshogs): byang chub sems dpa' ma yin do// de ci'i brir zhe na/ de dag ni sems can smyos pa zhes bya ba'i phyir ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa byang chung nam skyes shing / byang chub rlu
19b5(sna tshogs): du med pas/ byang chub kyi phyir sems par mi nus so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ de dag ni skye ba nyid la mngon par zhen kyang / de dag skye ba rab tu mi shes so//
19b6(sna tshogs): rang kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ skye ba mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa de ni yang dag pa nyid do// sems mnyam pa nyid gang yin pa dang / yang dag pa nyid gang yin pa dang / mnya
19b7(sna tshogs): pa nyid gang yin pa dang / yang dag pa nyid de ni byang chub ste/ gang na yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid yod pa de na rnam par rtog pa gang yang med ra/ de dag ni sems dang byang chub la rnam
20a1(sna tshogs): par brtags te/ gnyis su mngon par zhen nas// byang chub kyi phyir sems bskyed do// rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gdon bu/ sems kyang gzhan ma yin/
20a2(sna tshogs): byang chub kyang gzhan ma yin/ sems la byang chub med/ byang chub la'ang sems med de/ byang chub gang yin pa dang / sems gang yin pa de ni/ yang dag pa ji lta ba nyid dang /
20a3(sna tshogs): ji lta ba bzhin no// de la ni byang chub med/ sems kyang med // gang gi sems nyid dang / byang chub dang / skye ba dang / mi skye ba'ang mi dmigs pa de byang chub sems dpa'
20a4(sna tshogs): zhes bya'o// yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin gyi sems dpa' zhes bya'o// sems dpa' chen po zhes bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ des yang dag pa ma yin pa gang yin pa de shes
20a5(sna tshogs): pa'i phyir ro// yang dag pa ma yin pa gang zhe na/ 'jig rten thams cad ni yang dag pa ma yin pa ste/ yang dag pa ma yin par gartogs so// kye ma 'jig rten gnas pa 'di
20a6(sna tshogs): ni yang dag pa ma yin pa'o// ma byung ba'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa/ mi 'byung ba zhes bya zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa la 'byung ba gang yang med de
20a7(sna tshogs): yang dag pa ma yin pa ri mi 'byung ba'o// de'i phyir chos thams cad ngo bo nyid kyis med pa yang dag pa ma yin pa zhes bya'o// gang gis de ltar shes pa de ni/ yang dag par
20b1(sna tshogs): lta ba bzhin gyi se nus can zhes bya'o// yang dag pa la yang dag pa zhes mngon par mi zhen pas/ de'i phyir yang dag pa'i lta ba bzhin gyi sems can zhes bya ste/ ji gang du 'arjod
20b2(sna tshogs): ba bzhin du ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ yang dag pa ma yin pa la sems can nam/ sems can chen po zhes bya ba gang yang med pa'i phyir ro// gang gis rdeg pa chen rje
20b3(sna tshogs): khong du chud pa de sems can chen po zhes bya'o// theg pa chen po gang zhe na/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ni theg pa chen po'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes pa
20b4(sna tshogs): zhen gang ci'ang rung ste/ 'dus byas shes pa dang / 'dus ma byas shes pa dang / 'jog rten shes pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa shes pa des sems can chen po zhes
20b5(sna tshogs): d+ha'o/ de ci'i phyir zhen sems can du 'du shes pa chen po med pas de'i b+ha sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de lam rig pa'i phung po chen po med pas/ de'i phyir/
20b6(sna tshogs): sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de la 'du byed kyi phung po chen po med pasade'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de la phyi shes pa'i phung po chen po med pas
20b7(sna tshogs): de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// de la sdug bsngal gyi phung po chen po med pas/ de'i phyir sems can chen po zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod
21a1(sna tshogs): pa gang dag sems dpa' chen po'i 'du shes la'ang spongar la/ sems kyang mi dmigs sems las byung ba'i chos dang / sems kyi rang bzhin yang
21a2(sna tshogs): rab tu mi shes byang chub kyang mi dmigs/ byang chub kyi phyogs kyi chos rnams dang / byang chub kyi rang bzhin yang rab tu mi shes te/ de dag mi shes pa'i sems kyi byang chub kyang
21a3(sna tshogs): mi mthong / byang chub ma gtogs par sems kyang mi mthong / byang chub la sems mi mthong / sems la byang chub mi mthong ste/ gang de ltar rnam par 'jig pa de ni sgom pa'ang med
21a4(sna tshogs): rnam par 'jig par byed pa'ang myed de/ rnam par 'jig par byed pa de'ang mi dmigs shing / rlom sems mi byed la/ mngon par zhen pa de dag byang chub tu sems skyed do/
21a5(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang de ltar byang chub tu sems skyed pa de dag ri/ byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya ste/ de dag byang chub las phyir mi ldog go/
21a6(sna tshogs): de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang dag 'di ltar byang chub dang / sems dang / skye ba dang / 'gog pa tha dad du bya bar yang dag par rjes su mi mthong ba de dag byang chub nyid la gnas/
21a7(sna tshogs): pa ste 'di ni gang yang dag par rjes su mi mthong / gang la'ang mngon par mi zhe na/ gang la'ang rnam par rtog par mi 'gyur te/ rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa / gang
21b1(sna tshogs): dang de slar rnam par grol ba dang / rnam par grol bar sems mi skyed pa de dag ni/ byang drung sems dpa' yang dag pa zhes bya'o// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par brjod pa
21b2(sna tshogs): gang dag sems can du 'du shes pa dang / byang chub tu 'du shes pa dang / byang chub kyi phyirare sems skyed na/ de dag ni byang chub las ring ste/ de ni byang chub dang nye ma
21b3(sna tshogs): yin no// rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag byang chub las ring ba 'am/ nye bar yang dag paro rjes su mi mthong ba de dag byang chub dang nye ba ste/ de ni byang chub kyi phyir
21b4(sna tshogs): sems bskyed pa'o// rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par gnon pa/ ngas de la dgongs nas/ gang bdag gnyis su med par shes pa de ni/ sangs rgyas dang chos kyang rab tu shes so/
21b5(sna tshogs): zhes bshod do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gnyis su med pa yongs su shes pas/ chos thams cad yongs su shes te/ de chos thams cad kyi bdag gi ngo bo nyid sgom pa'i phyir ro//
21b6(sna tshogs): gang gnyis su med pa'i chos shes bya ba de ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos shes pa ste/ chos gnyis su med par yongs su shes pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su shes so//
21b7(sna tshogs): bdag yongs su shes pas/ khams gsum thams cad yongs su shes so// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gang dag yongs su shes pa zhes bya ba de ni/ chos thams
22a1(sna tshogs): cad kyi pha rol lo// chos thams cad kyi pha rol yang gang zhe na/ gang pha rol nyid kyang mi dmigs pha rol tu rlom sems su mi byed/ pha rol la
22a2(sna tshogs): mngon par mi zhen pa de ni/ yongs su shes pas pha rol tu song ba zhes bya ste/ ji skad du brjod pa bzhin du ni ma yin ro// rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ de ltar 'di ni blang
22a3(sna tshogs): chub sems dpa'i sa yin par rig par du'o// gang la shes par bya ba dang / rtogs par bya ba phra rab tsam yang med pa de ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ste/
22a4(sna tshogs): de la ni 'ong ba 'am/ 'gro ba mi mngon no// gleng gzhi'i le'u zhes bya ste dang po'o// / dam po gnyis pa/ de nas bcom ldan 'das la
22a5(sna tshogs): tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bos 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das nga rgyal can mtshan ma la spyod pa rnams bstan pa 'di la skrag par 'gyur lags so// de nas tshe dang ldan pa shwa ra dwa
22a6(sna tshogs): ti'i bus/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo la 'di skad ces smras so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi yul ma yin/ rtogs pa ma yin pas de dag 'di la
22a7(sna tshogs): skrag par mi 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ gang sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu song ba de dag ni 'di la skrag par gyur zin pas/ 'di ni de dag gi yul ma zhing ma rtogs so// tshe dang
22b1(sna tshogs): ldan pa kun dga' bo// gang dag nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir zhugs shing / nga rgyal spong ba'i phyir dartson pa de dag ni 'di la skrag par 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ du rgyal lo/
22b2(sna tshogs): du shes pas/ nga rgyal med pa tshol zhing nga rgyal spong ba tshul ba'i phyir ro// tshe dang ldan pa kun dka' bo/ gang dag nga rgyal mi dmigs shing yang dag par mi mthong la
22b3(sna tshogs): rlom sems su mi byed cing mngon par mi zhon pa de dag ni gang la'ang mi skrag/ gang le'ang mi de dang / gang la'ang dngang bar mi 'gyur ro// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo
22b4(sna tshogs): nga rgyal can rnams kyi phyi'i chosra bstan pa 'di zhus pa ma yin no// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni nga rgyal can rnams kyi yul ma yin te/ go skabs med do// gang dgang
22b5(sna tshogs): rgyal sbyong ba'i phyir brtson zhing 'bad pa de dag ni/ yang dag par 'bad pa me yin no// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nga rgyal zhes bya ba de ni/ lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs
22b6(sna tshogs): pa'i tshig bla dgas so// gang dag nga rgyal la spyor cing lhag par byed pa sgro 'dogs par byed pa de dag ni mtshungs par mi spyod do// mtshungs par spyod pa'ang ches 'di la
22b7(sna tshogs): be tsom za'o// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ gang dag mnyam pa'ang mi dmigs/ mi mnyam pa'ang ma yin/ mnyam par yang rlo mo sems mo byed/ mi mnyam par
23a1(sna tshogs): yang ma yin/ mnyam par yang mngon par mi zhen/ mi mnyam par yang ma yin pa de dag ni/ gang la'ang mi skrag/ mi dngang / da ngang bar mi 'gyur ro//
23a2(sna tshogs): tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ 'di ni byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad kyi yul ma yin te/ mi rtogs so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dge' bo/ 'di ni byis pa so so'i skye bo thams cad
23a3(sna tshogs): kyis shes shing rtogs pa ma yin no// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nyan thos kyi theg pa can rnams kyis kyang mi rtogs so// 'di ni gang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa can chos zab mo
23a4(sna tshogs): la spyod pa de dag gis kyang mi rtogs so// tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can gang dag mtshan ma la spyod pa/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis yongs
23a5(sna tshogs): su ma zir pa/ sdig pa'i grogs po'i lag tu song ba de dag kyang / chags pa med pa'i chos 'di dag mi rtogs shing yul ma yin te/ tshe dang ldan pa kun dga' bo/ nyan thos kyi
23a6(sna tshogs): theg pa can bden pa mthong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa can dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis bstan pa/ chos zab mo la mos pa/ gang chos 'di dag la 'thun par spyod pa
23a7(sna tshogs): dang gang chos 'di khong du chud cing / spyod pa rnams ni ma rtogs/ kun dga' bo/ byang chub sems dpa' mtshan ma dang bral ba/ mtshan ma med pa la spyod pa/ sna
23b1(sna tshogs): tshogs rnyed pal spyod pa/ zab mo'i chos shin tu mthar phyin pa/ gang dug sems dang byang chub sdud mi dmigs shing chos gang yang tha da du mi byed la/ yang dag par rjes
23b2(sna tshogs): su mi mthong ba ng+ge dag ni 'di lta bu'i chos la rmongs par mi 'gyur/ the tsom mi nga'o// ci'i phyir zhen/ de drug chos thams cad dang rjes su 'thun pa gnas te/
23b3(sna tshogs): mthun par ni ma yin pa'i phyir ro// de dag gis gang dang gang la chos 'dri ba de dang des rjes su 'thun par lan 'debs shing / rjes su 'thun par smra bar byed do// de
23b4(sna tshogs): nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa ku dga' bo la 'di skad ces bka' stsal te/ kun dga' bo ji ltar shA ri'i bu 'dis bshad pa de de bzhin te/ kun dga' bo chos bstan
23b5(sna tshogs): pa 'di dang / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub dang rjes su 'thun pa'i sangs rgyas kyi byang chub 'di ni/ nga rgyal can rnams kyi sa ma yin/ 'jug pa'i yul ma yin te/ kun dga' bo
23b6(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya chen po la ri dman pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems mi 'jug go// kun dga' bo/ dman pa la mos pa nga rgyal can rnams ni nga rgyal gyi dbang gis 'gro ngas/
23b7(sna tshogs): de dag sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la mi mthun par gnas so// kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di ni gtsang mo ste/ sngon gyi rgyal ba rnams la bya ba byas shing / dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/
24a1(sna tshogs): sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ zab mo la mos pa/ zab mo spyod pa ste/ kun dga' bo/ 'khor ba de la de bzhin gshegs pas yid bstan nas
24a2(sna tshogs): chos mngon par ston gyis/ rjes su srung ba'i chos ni cung zad kyang mi ston no// kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di ni snying po ste/ sa zhag dang / gseg ma dang / gyo mo med pa sangs
24a3(sna tshogs): rgyas brgya stong mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ snying po la rab tu gnas pa'o// kun dga' bo/ gseg ma dang gyo mo zhes bya ba de ni byis pa so so'i skye bo rnams kyi chog bla dgas te/ gang
24a4(sna tshogs): dgra chos 'di la go skabs med pa'o// kun dga' bo/ sa zhag ces bya ba 'di ni// sems can nga rgyal can rnams kyi tshig bla dgas so// kun dga' bo/ 'khor 'di ni nga rgyal med pa
24a5(sna tshogs): dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos mngon par 'phags pa'o// kun dga' bo/ 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i rgyal po ma dros pa rab tu dga' bar gyur te/ dga' ba dang yid bde ba skyes nas
24a6(sna tshogs): rang gi gnas na 'dod pa'i yod tan lnga spyod cing / rang gi gnas na rab tu dga' bar yang lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i char pa'i chu chen po 'bebs so// de'i bur gyur pa de dag kyang
24a7(sna tshogs): rab tu dga' nas/ rang rang gi gnas na 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga 'byor cing ldan par gyur te/ rtse zhing char chen po 'bebs so// kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs
24b1(sna tshogs): du 'acom pa spang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyang chos kyi char chen po 'bebs so// gang sras bu 'o byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag du/ 'a
24b2(sna tshogs): rten gyi 'ams 'di nas rang rang gi sangs rgyas kyi zhing du song ste/ chos kun 'byung ba 'di la brtsams nas de bzhin gshegs pa de dag gi sbyar sngar chos kyi char chen po gtong 'ang
24b3(sna tshogs): chos kyi chur chen po rab tu 'bebs so// kun dga' bo/ 'di lta ste/ dper na klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshon/ gang gi tshe rab tu dga' bar gyur pa de'i tshe/ rang gi gnas nas char gyi
24b4(sna tshogs): rgyun chen po 'bebs so// gang dag gnas dra na gnas par gyur pa'i klu de dag gis kyang char gyi rgyun de mnos nas dga' bar gyur te/ char gyi rgur des bde bar shes so// gang nga/
24b5(sna tshogs): ngo'i bur gyur pa de dag kyangachar gyi rgyun de brjod cing / char gyi rgyud des mchog tu dga' ba thib bo// de ci'i phyir zhe nu// kun dga' bo// kluganan dag gis char gyi rgyun de kyi
24b6(sna tshogs): bzod la/ klu gzhan drug ni char gyi rgyud des bde bar mi shes shing / char gyi rgyun de dag gis dga' bar mi 'gyur ba'i phyir ro// kun dga' bo de bzhin du/ gang dag de bzhin
24b7(sna tshogs): gshegs pa'i chos dkon mchog la lhag par chags pa dang / gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras thu bo byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dge ba'i rtsa ba byas pa/
25a1(sna tshogs): bsam pa rgya che ba chos zab mo'i tshul las nges par skyes pa de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi tshul gyi char chen po 'di bzod do// thos nas rab tu
25a2(sna tshogs): dga' zhing mgu ste bde bar shes so// kun dga' bo// de bzhin gshegs pas don gyi dbang 'di la brten te/ bsam pa dag pa'i 'khor du seng ge'i sgra chen po sgrog cing / chos kyi
25a3(sna tshogs): char chen po 'bebs so// kun dga' bo// 'di lta ste/ dper na 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po rin po che'i mdzod mang po bsam pa dang ldan pa des/ bu mang po rigs dang ldan zhing /
25a4(sna tshogs): rgyud kyis kyang dag pa de dag thams cad bkug nas rin po che'i mdzod bgos te/ bu gang la'ang mi bsla bar byin no// de ltar bgos pa de dag 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po de dga' ba dang /
25a5(sna tshogs): mgu ba chen po lhag par skyes nas/ 'khor lo sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang don mtshungs par gyur to snyam ste/ bdag bde bar shes so// kun dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa
25a6(sna tshogs): chos kyi rgyal po// chos kyi bdag po rang byung gis kyang sras de dag bsdus nas/ chos rin po che'i mdzod 'di mnyam par bgos te/ sras de dag gang la'ang mi smra bas
25a7(sna tshogs): dag gang la dga' ba dang / mgu ba dang / gus pa cher skyed cing / don mthun pa sangs rgyas kyi rigs mi gcod par gnas so// kun dga' bo/ sems can gzhan dman pa
25b1(sna tshogs): 'os pa/ darnal pa lta ba la spyod bya/ mtshan ma la spyod pa/ dmigs pa la spyod pa/ da'o smras pa'i nga rgyal gyis bcom pa/ 'dod chags dang / de
25b2(sna tshogs): drug pal gyis gnan gyi/ sa par 'am du ring pa rnams kyis chos rin po che 'di bsod par ma nus s+ho// dgyur ro// dman pa la mos pa'i sems ca rnams
25b3(sna tshogs): 'a'adzilo gyur dab ror ma 'dod kyi/ kun dga' bo/ gang dga' bor lo sgyur ba'i bur gyur pa de dag ni/ 'khor la sgyur ba'i nor 'dod do// kun dga' bo/ sems can dngus
25b4(sna tshogs): ma dang po nga / glang po 'an po che dang / ri po me nor bu dang po che dang / dring med rin po rje dang khyim bdag rin po che dang /

25b7(sna tshogs): de ga ring po che la mi mkhas pa'i phyir ro// kun dga' bo/ sems cin dbul po ni rin po che 'di'i ming ni 'di'o zhes bya bar rin po che rnams kyi ming yang mi shes so// kun
26a1(sna tshogs): dga' bo de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sras bder pa mthong ba rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag ri/ chos ringan po che'i mdzod
26a2(sna tshogs): 'a tshal ba ste/ chos rin po che dmigs su med pa/ stong pa nyid dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos dang ldan bu 'di 'dod cing bzod de/ de dag des bya ba byed do// sems
26a3(sna tshogs): car dbul po thos pa dang bral ba/ thos pa nyams pa/ mig dang mi ldan pa'i byis pa de dag ni/ chos ri po che'i mdzod rnyed kyang ci zhig bya zhes 'dor zhing / gzhan la
26a4(sna tshogs): sbyin par sems so// kun dga' bo// gdol pa dang / g.yung po dang / sgyu ma mkhan dang / dbul pos 'tshe ba'i sems can gang gzhan la las rin po che'i mdzod rnyed
26a5(sna tshogs): na bdag mi spyod de/ rin thang chung ngur 'tshong zhing 'dor ro// kun dga' bo/ sems cad dbul po zhes bya ba de ni mu stegs can thams cad dang / gang dag mu stegs car gyi/
26a6(sna tshogs): nyan thos rnams kyi tshig bla dgas so// kun dga' bo/ sems cad dbul po zhes bya ba de ni byis pa so so'i skye bo lta ba'i 'dam du bying ba/ dmigs pa can/ 'ching ba/
26a7(sna tshogs): la mngon par zhen pa mtshan ma la spyod pa/ lam log par song ba rnams kyi tshig bla dgas te/ de dag ni chos rin po che 'di rI da na kun tu spyod mi rus shing 'dor te/
26b1(sna tshogs): k+Sha Ang sbyi ba d+hA de/ sa su rgya / smra rnams spyod yul la sma pa shegs rnaM kum+b+ha
26b2(sna tshogs): ba gnas pa de dag rin po che 'di la yongs su spyod do// rnyed nas kyang chud pa gson cid/ 'di la rin po cher 'du shes 'gyur ro// kun dka' bo// lus ni sri kI'i sgra rlog+sa
26b3(sna tshogs): mi nus so// kur dka' ro// klang seng ki'i drug sur gyur la/ snying ka chen pos bskyed par dag seng ge'i sgyu zlog go// kun dga' rdo de bzhin du la lhun ni byis pa so so'i skye ba 'o/
26b4(sna tshogs): par lta ba thams cad de/ de dag gis ri de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i sgra dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas song gi chen po'i chos yongs su 'angs spyod par mi nus so// un
26b5(sna tshogs): dka' 'o// gang yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sras sangs rgyas kyi seng ge chen po dang / rang byung gi ye shes kyis bskyed pa dag ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi seng ge'i
26b6(sna tshogs): sgra sgrog cing kun tu stong do// de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ tshe dang ldan pa shA ra dwa tI'i dus 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs
26b7(sna tshogs): de'i 'khor yongs su dag pa 'dus pa 'di ngo mtshar to// bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor/ rang byung gi 'khor/ mi tshugs pa'i 'khor rdo rje lta bu'i 'a
27a1(sna tshogs): mi bskul pa/ mi bskyod pa/ mi 'khrugs pa'i 'khor yongs su dag pa 'di ni rab tu ngo mtshar lags so// de skad ces gsol pa dang / bcom ldan
27a2(sna tshogs): 'das kyis/ tshe dang ldan pa sh+tsa ra da ti'i bul 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// shwa ri'i buM/ khyod 'khor 'di'i yon tan yongs su brjod dam/ gsol pa/ bcom ldan 'das
27a3(sna tshogs): bdag gis 'khor 'di'o yon tan yongs su brjod pa'i rngo mi thogs lags so// de ci'i slad du zhe na/ bcom ldan 'das 'khor 'di ni ro rab dang 'dra ste/ yon tan mtha' yas pa
27a4(sna tshogs): dang ldan pa lags pa'i slad du'o// bka' stsal pa/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu de de bzhin te/ 'khor 'di na yod tar mtha' yas pa dang ldan pa ste/ 'khor 'di'i yon tan gyi mtha'
27a5(sna tshogs): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis kyang rtogs par mi nus na/ sems cad gzhan thams cad kyis lta ci spos/ shA ra dwa ti'i bu/ de bzhin gshegs pas bslus pa
27a6(sna tshogs): ma yid zhing / 'di la de bzhir gshegs pas rtsol ba ci'ang mi mdzad de/ rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas/ nga'i ming thos nas 'khor 'dir 'dus te/ de bzhin gshegs pas 'khor 'di
27a7(sna tshogs): ga la'ang ma glengs ma bsgo bar de dag rang gi dge ba'i rtsa bas bskul nas 'khor 'dir lpags so// 'di lta bu'i chos bstan pa la/ 'di lta bu'i sems can chen po 'du bar 'gyur
27b1(sna tshogs): nI ri'i chos do// shA ra dwa ti'i bu / gang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gzhan dag byang chub sems dpa'i sde stong gi rtsom thams cad gcod pa 'ang ya dag par sto pa de dag gi 'a'
27b2(sna tshogs): 'di lta bu 'du bar 'gyur te/ de lta bu 'ang 'dra ba'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor gdon mi za bar 'byung ba ni chos bstan pa 'di'i chos nyid do// kun dga' bo'i le'u zhes bya ste gnyis pa'o//
27b3(sna tshogs): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa la bka' stsal pa/ rab kyi rdul gyis rnam par garten pa/ shes
27b4(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa zhes bya ba la/ byang chub sems dpa'i shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gang zhe na/ gang chos thams cad kyi tshu rol rtogs pa ste/
27b5(sna tshogs): de ni bsten par mi nus mod kyi/ ji ltar khyed shes par 'gyur ba dang / ji ltar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tha snyad kyi tshig tu 'gyur ba de ltar rab tu bshad par bya'o// gzugs shes
27b6(sna tshogs): rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa gzugs las gzhan pa'ang ma yin no// de bzhin du sbyar te/ de ltar tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang
27b7(sna tshogs): 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ma yin te/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rnam par shes pa las gzhan pa'ang ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/
28a1(sna tshogs): rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par gnon pa/ gzugs kyi pha rol gang yin pa de gzugs ma yin la/ de bzhin du sbyar te/ de ltar tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang /
28a2(sna tshogs): 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa'i pha rol gang yin pa rnam par shes pa ma yin pa'i phyir ro// gzugs kyi pha rol ji lta bar gzugs kyang dri bzhin no// de bzhin du tshor ba
28a3(sna tshogs): dang 'du shes dang / 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar rnam par shes pa'ang de bzhin no// rnam par shes pa'i pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad
28a4(sna tshogs): kyang de bzhin no// chos thams cad kyi pha rol grang yin pa de dag ni chos thams cad ma yin no// chos thams cad kyi pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin no// rab kyi
28a5(sna tshogs): rtsal gyis rnam par gnod pa/ de la gzugs kyi pha rol gang yin pa de gzugs ma yin no// zhes bya ba de ni gzugs kyi 'bral ba bstan pa'o// gzugs kyi pha rol ji lta bar
28a6(sna tshogs): gzugs kyang de bzhin no/ zhes bya ba de ni gzugs kyi ngo bo nyid bshad pa bstan pa'o// de ni gzugs kyi ji lta ba bzhin bstan pa'o// de ni gzugs kyi rang bzhir bstan pa'o//
28a7(sna tshogs): de ni gzugs kyi mi dmigs pa bstan pa'o// de bzhin du tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed rnams dang / rnam par shes pa'i pha rol gang yin pa de rnam par shes pa ma yin
28b1(sna tshogs): ro// zhus bya ba de ni dam par shes da'i 'bral ba bgyur pa'o// rnam pa shes pa'i 'o lta ba rnam par shes pa'ang de babyin na/ zhes bya ba ni rnam par shes pazung ba d+ma bshang ba
28b2(sna tshogs): bsnyen da'o// de ni rnam par shes pa'i ji lta ba bzhin dang / rnam par shes pa'i rang bzhin dang / rnam par shes pa'i mi dmigs pa bstan pa'o// rnam par shes pa'i pha ro
28b3(sna tshogs): lhu bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin do zhes bya ba dang / chos thams cad kyi pha rol gang yin pa de dag chos thams cad ma yin no// zhes kyi ba de ni chos thams cad kyi 'bral ba bstan pa'o/
28b4(sna tshogs): chos thams cad kyi pha rol ji lta bar chos thams cad kyang de bzhin no// zhes bya ba de ni chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid bshad pa bstan pa'o// de ni chos thams cad kyi ji lta ba bzhin dang
28b5(sna tshogs): chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang / chos thams cad kyi mi dmigs pa bstan pa'o// chos thams cad kyi ji lta ba bzhin dang / chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang / chos thams cad kyi mi
28b6(sna tshogs): dmigs pa ji lta bar shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang de bzhin te/ rab kyi rdul gyi rnam par gnon pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gzugs la mi gnas so// tshor ba dang / 'du

30b1(sna tshogs): 'gyur 'du 'phel bar 'gyur ba ma yin no// de bzhin du tshor ba dang / 'du shes dang / 'du byed rnams dang rnam pa shes pa'ang 'bribar 'gyur ba du/

64b1(sna tshogs): ma ga pa 'dugang dag gi rnalas du thos pa'i sems sa de sa kyang dag pa'i rtsa bcung ngu dang ldan pa ma yin na/ gang dag 'dzin pa dang / 'anang 'du sa padang ra du

64b4(sna tshogs): med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub la 'dun pa skyed par 'gyur ba de dag gi chos bstan pa'ang de nyid yin no// de ci'i phyir phrin shA ri'i bu sems can gang dag chos rab mo thos

64b7(sna tshogs): gang dag gi rna lam du thos par 'gyur ba dang / thos nas klog pa dang / mos pa dang / dga' ba dang yid bde ba chen po spyad pa dang phyi zhing nyan pa'i phyir chos 'di la 'dun pa
65a1(sna tshogs): skyed pa'i sems can de dag kyang 'khor ba chen por zhugs par ngas ma bshad ra lung nod pa dang kha ton byed pa dang gzhan la ston pa lta ci smos
65a2(sna tshogs): shA ri'i bu nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la nges par 'gyur bar ma zhugs shing ma nges pa ni ngas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan to// shA ri'i bu/

65b1(sna tshogs): bar pa dang bde ba'i phyir zhugs pa snang babyed pa sems can rnams kyi bu stegs su gyur ba snying rje chen po dang ldan pa par bar snying brtse ba phan par 'dong ba da
65b2(sna tshogs): bar 'dod pa/ grub pa dang bde bar 'dod pa/ sems can thams cad la bde bar sbyar bar nye bar gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de lta bu de dag gi nor chen po yid do//

66a1(sna tshogs): na rlung gi khams kyi yul dang spyod yul ni mtha' yas so// de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i yul drang spyod yul yang mtha' yas so// shA ri'i bu
66a2(sna tshogs): 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha'i khams kyi yul dang spyod yul ni mtha' yas so// de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i yul dang spyod yul ni nam mkha' 'o// shA ri'i bu/

66a4(sna tshogs): bu 'di lta ste/ dper na nam mkha'i khams dang / rlung gi khams ni/ gang na'ang mi snang zhing / chos grang mngon par grub pa'i mtshan nyid du'ang nye bar gnas pa ma yin no//
66a5(sna tshogs): shA ri'i bu de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'ang chos gang la'ang mi snang zhing chos gang mngon par grub pa'i mtshan nyid du'ang nye bar gnas pa ma yin no// shA ri'i du 'di lta ste/

66b1(sna tshogs): rnarnam pa pa'i 'ams dang / rlung mas ni chos gang yongs su grub par mthong bar che bar 'gro ba ma yin no// de bzhin du shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyir pa'ang chos gang yongs su grub dur brjong

67a1(sna tshogs): chags pa med pa zhes bya ba de ni chags pa yongs su shes pa'o// de ni chags pa mi dmigs pa'o// de ni chags pa'i yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin no// de ni chags

68b7(sna tshogs): skye bo rnams ri ma yin no// shA ri'i bu shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa 'di ni dmin pa la mos pa'i sems can rnams kyi lag tu 'gro bar mi 'gyur gyi shA ri'i bu/
69a1(sna tshogs): shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bstan pa 'di ni sems can gang dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su dag pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa de dag gi lag tu

69a5(sna tshogs): ngag lung bstan pa de dag kyang myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur te/ smon lam gyi dbang gis ni ma gtogs so// gang dag lung ma bstan

69a7(sna tshogs): pa nyid du rig par byen/ gang mdi sde 'di rnyed pa dang / yi ger 'dri ba dang / 'chang ba dang / lung nod pa dang / kha ton byed pa dang / gzhan la'ang rgya cher rab tu ston pa lta ci smos/

70a1(sna tshogs): 'bras bu ni 'di ma yin te/ gang byang chub sems dpa' dang nyan thos 'di lta bu'i chos thos na/ bag med par mi 'gyur ba dang yid ston par mi 'gyur ba
70a2(sna tshogs): dang / 'dud pa yongs su nyams pa dang / brtson 'grus bri ba dang / ma grims pa ston pa dang / gnod sems mang du 'gyur ba de ni thos pa'i 'bras bu ma yin no// de dag gis
70a3(sna tshogs): 'di lta bu'i chos 'di thos pa ma yin no// shA ri'i bu/ thos shes bya ba de ni yang dag pa'i nan tanar gyi tshig bla dgas te/ log pa'i na tar gyi ma yin no// sha ri'i bu log
70a4(sna tshogs): par zhugs pas ni/ chos 'di thos par mi 'gyur ro// shA ri'i bu/ thos nas khyod don la mkhas shing nan tan gyis gnas par bya'o// shA ri'i bu log par zhugs
70a5(sna tshogs): pa rnams la rjes su 'thun pa'i bzod pa'ang med do// shA ri'i bu/ gang ji skad bstan pa'i chos 'di la log par mi sgrub pa de ni/ chos 'di la nan tan byed pa zhes bya'o// shA ri'i bu/
70a6(sna tshogs): bzod pa phun sum tshogs pa'i gang zag nan tan la gnas pa dag ni phyir ngan song du 'gro bar mi 'gyur gyi/ myur du chos 'di yang dag par sgrub par 'gyur ro// dge ba'i rtsa ba dang ngor
70a7(sna tshogs): tsa ma la yid brtan par mi bya ste/ chos 'di yongs su ma grub kyi bar du brtson pa mi gtong ba'ang yid brtan par mi bya'o// shA ri'i bu/ gang chos 'di bslabs pa dang / yongs su

70b3(sna tshogs): byin sel ga las byung ste yang dag pa ma yid pa'o// zhes yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du mthod pa yin no// de ltar yang dag pa thong bde ni 'apyod pa dran sa ma myogs pa
